Each set contains 7 entries.
Number of bits used for the index is 6.

Number of virtual pages is 16.
Number of physical pages is 8.
Each page contains 16384 bytes.

Number of bits used for the page offset is 14.

D-cache contains 64 sets.
Each set contains 7 entries.
Each line is 1024 bytes.
The cache uses a no write-allocate and write-through policy.

Number of bits used for the offset is 10.

L2-cache contains 64 sets.
Each set contains 6 entries.
Each line is 1024 bytes.
The cache uses a write-allocate and write-back policy.

Number of bits used for the offset is 10.

L2 cache is disabled in this configuration.
